The Japanese Plan to Seize the Rights of the Eastern Railway

Iri Haru Appointed as Fake Director

The Harbin-Suifenhe Line Divided into Several Sections

The Puppet State Plans to Revise the Agreement

Harbin Correspondence: Since the Eastern Railway was incorporated into the transportation system of the puppet state, the old Japanese personnel have been almost completely ousted. Li Shaogeng, the puppet superintendent, is in a position where he must act, but he does not seem willing to be a puppet. If Li does not act, his property in Harbin, worth hundreds of thousands, will be confiscated. But after he acts, only the superintendent's office is under his control. The directors, supervisors, and the railway bureau are all controlled by the general new nobles. It is difficult to control, and Li really has no way to deal with it. The position of Chinese Deputy Director of the Railway Bureau was recently filled by Iri Haru, the former director of the Economic Investigation Bureau of the Railway Bureau, who was recommended by the Manchurian group. Iri is from Xinjiang and does not speak or understand Chinese. When the puppet state was established, he and Zhang Shu, the chairman of the supervisory board of the Eastern Railway, formed a Manchurian group in Harbin, forming cliques for private gain. Many people who were keen on fame and fortune joined the group. Using this power, Iri obtained the position of Deputy Director of the Railway Bureau. Although Li Shaogeng opposed it, there was nothing he could do. Now, nine out of ten of the heads of the Railway Bureau have been replaced. Those with some technical knowledge in the past, if they were not from the Manchurian group, were all ousted. The newly appointed ones are all about eating and taking money, reporting small matters to Iri and major matters to the Japanese side. In reality, it is the same as the semi-Manchurian system. The Soviet Union has not expressed any opinion on this. What they are most concerned about at the moment is how to plunder the railway property and transport it to Russia. Since February, vehicles on the Harbin-Suifenhe line have only gone to Ashihe. At the furthest, they only went to Suifenhe. The traffic to Vladivostok has long been cut off. Since the Soviet Union does not pay attention to railway matters, it is not eager to restore the entire Harbin-Suifenhe line. As a result, railway operations are fragmented, opening an unprecedented era of chaos. The Russians turn a blind eye to it. Recently, the section of the Harbin-Suifenhe line between Hengdaohe and Yimianpo has been directly managed by the Japanese army, and employees of the South Manchuria Railway and railway corps have been transferred to serve on the line. The Russian side does not dare to interfere. This section now belongs to the Japanese. The section above Hengdaohe, up to Suifenhe, is managed by the National Salvation Army. All daily traffic is controlled by the army. The area between Ashihe and Yimianpo is the most chaotic. Because the self-defense army uses the terrain for combat, many sections of the railway have been dismantled, and traffic is intermittent. The Russians can do nothing about it. This belongs to the problems of the railway itself. Recently, the Japanese want to bring the Eastern Railway under their control, as the entire Northeast has already been conquered. However, they cannot directly speak out, so they manipulate the puppet state's Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Ministry of Transportation to instruct Li Shaogeng, the superintendent of the Eastern Railway, to propose to the Russian directors and supervisors to revise all or part of the Sino-Russian and Fengtian-Russian agreements (specifically referring to the Eastern Railway portion) and to return the Eastern Railway passenger and freight cars and property detained in the Soviet Union. Japan Threatens the League of Nations that It Will Not Recognize the General Assembly

Opposes the League of Nations' Application of Article 15

Instructs the Plenipotentiary to Communicate with the Powers

The Osaka Asahi Shimbun reports that the League of Nations General Assembly, originally scheduled to be held in September, has been changed to November. It is expected that Japan's opposition to the General Assembly will be serious. At present, the Japanese government's attitude is still proceeding according to the established policy. If the League of Nations invokes Article 15 of the Covenant regarding the Manchurian Incident, Japan will resolutely not recognize the General Assembly. However, in order to prevent a head-on confrontation, the government has instructed the Japanese plenipotentiary representative in Geneva to make every effort to communicate with the representatives of the major powers, stating Japan's attitude: (1) Japan will never change its established policy and invoke Article 15; (2) Japan believes that the handling of the Sino-Japanese dispute falls within the scope of the Council's authority, and the General Assembly has no right to deliberate. Japan believes that it is inappropriate for the Council to transfer all disputes to the General Assembly for handling; (3) At the same time, Japan will reserve its attendance at the General Assembly. After the Council accepts the report of the Commission of Inquiry and continues to deliberate, if there are actions unfavorable to Japan in the future solution, or if it denies the existence of Manchuria, a major conflict will inevitably occur.

The Bandit Situation in Eastern Fujian is Rampant

The Tea Market Center is Captured

The Fish Market Center is Surrounded

Fuzhou Correspondence: The authorities of this province, recently preoccupied with dealing with the red bandits in southern and northern Fujian, have only dispatched the Second Brigade of the Marine Corps, led by Lin Bingzhao, to garrison the five coastal counties of Funing Prefecture in eastern Fujian: Ningde, Xiapu, Fuan, Shouning, and Fuding. However, Lin's brigade pays no attention to local defense and only focuses on forcing the planting of opium seedlings and levying donations. Farmers who resist are massacred by the dispatched troops, resulting in tragic incidents. The local groups jointly appealed to the central government, and the Military Affairs Commission telegraphed the provincial government a few days ago, ordering it to investigate and reply truthfully for investigation and handling. While the military and civilians are still in stalemate, the bandits have taken this opportunity to become active, and the most powerful forces include three groups: one is Li Mugong's group, which is active in the coastal counties of Xiapu and Fuan; one is Zhou Yuguang's group, which appears and disappears in the border areas of Fujian and Zhejiang, in the counties of Shouning and Fuding; and one is Xu Meiling's group, which loots the inland counties of Ningde and Pingnan in Ning Prefecture. Each group has more than a thousand members and runs rampant in one area. The army and the bandits seem to have concluded a non-aggression treaty, and they all choose to station themselves in areas without bandits, leaving the people to appeal. Funing is an area in Fujian Province that produces tea and fish. Now that the tea season has begun and the fish are abundant, it is a crucial time for the livelihood of both farmers and merchants throughout the year. The bandit forces are also very rampant. Li and Xu's groups are united as one, with about 2,000 people. They have captured the three towns of Baishi, Xiuxi, and Shuiteng, which are the tea market centers of Fuan and Xiapu counties, one after another. The tea leaves picked by the farmers and the cash carried by the merchants for tea were all looted. Now they are attacking Saiqi, the fish market center of Ning Prefecture, and it is already surrounded, and the situation is very critical. At the same time, the county seat of Shouning has also been captured by Zhou's bandits. Even the San Dou Island commercial port, where the headquarters of the Marine Corps is located, has had its water traffic cut off by bandit ships. The routes between the five counties have been completely cut off. The Funing Prefecture Association of Fellow Provincials, seeing that their hometown is in a state of ruin, specially selected representatives to petition the provincial government yesterday, requesting that warships be dispatched quickly to cooperate with the land troops to suppress the bandits. The Funing Tea Industry Association also sent a telegram to the province, stating that the entire tea market in the east has been destroyed and requesting prompt relief. It is unknown what the provincial government will do. (June 20th)

The Passenger and Cargo Ships Between Datong and Wuhu Are Robbed Again

Wuhu Correspondence: Chen's 57th Division in Xuancheng, Langxi, Guangde, Datong, and Wuhu in Anhui Province has been ordered to move to the border areas of the Gan Province. The Military Affairs Commission has specially transferred the officer training corps of the Central Military Academy to Anhui Province to fill the defense. The corps headquarters led one battalion to stay in Wuhu, and one battalion was sent to Datong and Xuancheng. The military police inspection office was reorganized, and the corps adjutant Ma Qingfeng was appointed as the director. The inns and hotels in the port will be thoroughly investigated. The corps commander Zhu Zonghai went to the provincial capital on the 23rd because it was necessary to discuss various matters with the provincial authorities after taking over the defense. The 57th Division Commander Li Songshan went to Beijing on the morning of the 22nd to meet with Chen Diaoyuan to ask for instructions on everything, as his troops were about to depart.

The merchant ships sailing to various places in Wuhu have been repeatedly robbed. On the 22nd, the Shenglong merchant ship, full of passengers and cargo from Datong, was robbed again on the way. The loss was about 2,000 yuan, but fortunately no one was injured. The ship arrived in Wuhu at 2:00 in the afternoon and, as usual, submitted a report to the military police authorities to request apprehension.

Disaster in Zheng County

Four Days of Wind and Frost

Severe Frost in the Morning, Wheat Is Burned

Kaifeng Correspondence: The Provincial Relief Association received a report from Liang Zihou, the magistrate of Zheng County, and Zhang Daoren, the district chief of the county's seventh district, stating that on the 11th of this month, a storm suddenly arose and lasted for four days and nights. Dust and sand filled the sky, and the daylight was dim. On the morning of the 15th, severe frost fell. On the highlands, the topsoil was blown away, and the wheat roots were completely exposed. In the lowlands, sand and leaves were rolled up and pressed on the wheat. In addition, severe frost fell, so that the green fields suddenly turned into scorched earth. Zheng has suffered from disasters and famines for years, and the people have struggled to eat. This spring, the wheat grew well, and there was hope for a good harvest, and starvation could be avoided. However, after the wind and frost, looking around the fields, the soil and seedlings were burned, and there was no hope for a harvest. Although there are seedlings that survive in the autumn, the harvest period is still far away, and it will not be enough to meet the immediate need. Moreover, drought and floods are uncertain, and it is difficult to expect an autumn harvest. Therefore, they earnestly request that personnel be sent to investigate and provide relief. A previous investigation report stated that the wind and frost disasters in the seven districts varied in severity. The report listed the number of acres affected by the disaster, with the severity differentiated. According to this, the winter in Zheng County was extremely dry, and less than 30% of the wheat was planted. Now, after the heavy wind and frost, the wheat blooms but does not bear fruit. The harvest in the whole county is less than 10% or 20%. At this time of year when the old crop is gone and the new crop has not yet arrived, how can my people bear this disaster? How should we reduce the land tax, plan relief, or use work as relief to make up for the damage? In addition to the county magistrate consulting with local gentry to find a solution, the details of the disaster have been submitted to the commission for review. It is said that after receiving the report, the Provincial Relief Association immediately telegraphed an appeal to raise relief efforts.

Communist Organization Smashed in Weixian, Shandong Province

Dozens of Communists Arrested

A visitor from Jinan said that Han Fuju, the chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, saw that the Communist bandits were rampant in the provinces of Jiangxi and Anhui and that Shandong was located in the middle, making it an important position. He specially ordered the military police under his command to strictly investigate and arrest the latent Communists in order to stabilize the local area. Previously, many Communists had been arrested in Jinan and Qufu and were detained for interrogation. Recently, Ma Guan's unit of the 222nd Brigade in Weixian County also smashed a Communist organization and arrested dozens of Communists, mostly school teachers and students. They are being interrogated at the brigade headquarters. It is said that they will be sent to Jinan in the near future to be handed over to the court for trial.

The Jiangsu Construction Department Telegraphed the Shandong Construction Department to Stop Dredging the River Alone

The Matter Concerns the Interests of Both Provinces and Requires Comprehensive Consideration

Recently, Shandong Province has independently managed the Grand Canal, dredging the East and West Si Rivers and the Niutou River to enter the Nanyang and Zhaoyang Lakes. The counties of Qian and Pei in Jiangsu are located downstream and cannot accommodate the sudden influx of excessive water, which will inevitably cause flooding. Therefore, the Pei County Government and the Tongshan County Farmers' Association have successively telegraphed the Jiangsu Construction Department for instructions. It is said that the department believes that the matter concerns the interests of both provinces and that unilateral water management without prior consultation is not a comprehensive consideration. Yesterday, it telegraphed the Shandong Construction Department, ordering it to stop the dredging work and to plan a mutually beneficial solution in order to avoid benefiting one and harming the other.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

The Red Cross Branch Distributes Relief Rice

Since being reorganized during the tense situation of the Songhu War, the Songjiang Red Cross Branch has been earnestly handling the reception of refugees and the relief efforts of the 43rd Injured Soldiers Hospital. Because Songjiang is close to the war zone, the general poor households have been affected by the war, and it is difficult to obtain food. The chairman of the branch, Zhou Xuewen, went to Shanghai to the Red Cross General Association and obtained permission to allocate 200 piculs of relief rice to be transported to Songjiang for distribution. A meeting was held at the headquarters on Malu Bridge to discuss the distribution methods. It was also resolved to first divide the area and conduct a field survey of the poor households. Once the household registers of each district are sent and reviewed, rice tickets will be issued to each household, and rice will be issued on a regular basis. In addition to appointing Zhou Xuewen, Zhu Jiuwang, Du Ruozhou, and Bai Tianyi as district directors, Zhang Shengshan, who has been in charge of the accounting for past relief efforts, was publicly elected as the accounting director to review everything. In the year of Dingmao, the association established a summer epidemic hospital, which was quite successful. Recently, in view of the severe epidemic this summer, which has been seen in various ports, it is feared that the infection will spread, and it is planned to gather comrades to continue to run the summer epidemic hospital. Zhou Xuewen, the chairman of the association, and others are planning everything, and they deeply hope that people from all walks of life will work together to promote and establish it as soon as possible. This is of great importance to public health.

The Aftermath of the Robbery in the Business District

After the Songjiang branch of the Chinese Industrial and Commercial Bank was robbed in broad daylight the other day, not only the financial community was filled with fear, but also the shops were on high alert. The County Chamber of Commerce held an informal discussion yesterday to make amends for the loss, and it was proposed to organize a special defense team in the city, recruiting 20 security guards. The funding will be 5,000 yuan as the standard, to be borne by various merchants and wealthy people. Yang Zhimin, Zhu Huisheng, and others were appointed as drafting members, Shu Baoshan and Zhang Shengshan as fundraising members, and Cai Zhongyu and Song Ruoyu as preparatory members. They will actively prepare immediately so that it can be established in the shortest possible time.

Qingpu

The Chonggu Patrol Officer is Accused

Recently, Zhu Shizhi, the district chief of the ninth district of the county, has reported to the county government and the county public security bureau that Chen Lianzhi, the patrol officer of the Chonggu branch office in the district, has neglected his duties and violated the law. The county government has instructed to investigate, and the county bureau has also sent Wang, a staff member, to the town for a thorough investigation.

Wuxi

Resolutely Oppose the Special Business Tax: The Jiangsu Provincial Government, facing significant debt due to financial difficulties, has introduced a special business tax. While the tax rates are classified into six categories, the specific items number over 360, sparking opposition from chambers of commerce in Shanghai, Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Zhenjiang, and trade associations such as the Wuxi Oil Factory and Grain Guild. The Jiangsu Provincial Federation of Commerce, after receiving requests from various county chambers of commerce to telegraph the Executive Yuan and Ministry of Finance to halt the tax, forwarded the request to the Yuan and Ministry. An explicit order to abolish the tax was issued. However, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, citing its dire financial situation, has not stopped the tax despite the Yuan's order and plans to implement it on July 1st. Several days ago, it summoned preparation members from various counties to the province to discuss the implementation procedures. Wang Xinru, the preparation member from Wuxi, also attended the meeting and submitted a detailed report on the taxable amount in Wuxi to the Department of Finance. However, merchants and residents of various counties believe that after years of famine and the impact of war, with financial stagnation and no reduction in various levies, and without government relief, it is impossible to bear further burdens. Therefore, they will fully oppose the special business tax, regardless of how the provincial government tries to collect it, even at the cost of everything. The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce, after receiving requests from various industries to convene an emergency meeting of all members, held an emergency meeting yesterday (the 24th) at 3 PM at the chamber. Qian Sunqing was elected as chairman to report on the process of repeatedly attending the Provincial Federation of Commerce to oppose the tax. Over 100 members attended and unanimously opposed the tax. The atmosphere at the meeting was very tense. There were two reasons for the opposition: (1) The implementation of the special business tax will inevitably lead to increased prices and a higher cost of living, potentially creating a situation similar to the terror in provinces like Fujian, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Anhui. (2) If the provincial government does not heed the explicit order of the Yuan and Ministry, merchants will not heed the explicit orders of the provincial government. The meeting concluded at 4:30 PM with three resolutions: (1) issue a circular telegram, (2) distribute a declaration, and (3) organize a Tax Rate Research Committee. Chen Zhanru, Chen Jinli, and Cheng Jingtang were appointed as committee members, to be convened by Chen Zhanru. The meeting then discussed the issue of clearing enemy goods as ordered, and resolved: (1) Various industries will take an oath on a set date to never purchase enemy goods again, (2) Jiang Jinghai and Jiang Hanqing were appointed as members of the Clearing Enemy Goods Committee, to be convened by Jiang Jinghai. The meeting then adjourned.

A Farmhouse Burglary in Jinqiao Township: Two households, Wei Peiquan and Wei Zhen'an, farmers from Weijia Lane, Cangqiao Township, Fifth District, were burglarized. At about 1 AM the day before yesterday, 13 bandits armed with pistols and other weapons scaled the wall and entered the Wei residence. The men and women of the Wei family were turned upside down and looted at will. 60 silver dollars, 6 silver ingots, 2 gold rings, 2 wooden boxes, and 1 rattan box were stolen, totaling over 700 yuan in losses. The next day, the victims reported the incident to the 13th sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau, which forwarded the report to the County Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Oil Firm Shareholder Accused of Embezzlement: The Wang Yuan Chang Oil Firm, located outside the North Gate along the river, is jointly owned by the brothers Wang Yaoqian, Wang Pushan, and Wang Baoshan. It is a large-scale operation with prosperous business. The accountant, Wang Jing, is the son of Wang Baoshan. Both father and son are keen on speculative ventures and often engage in private exchange transactions. However, due to years of failures and significant losses, they embezzled over 18,000 yuan from the firm. Recently, Wang Yaoqian and Wang Pushan discovered the embezzlement while auditing the accounts and filed a criminal lawsuit with the court. Wang Baoshan and his son went into hiding. Yesterday, Wang Jing was found and immediately handed over to the Fifth Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau, which transferred him to the County Court for interrogation. Furthermore, the Shen Changyuan Rice Firm in Chunyang Town, Jiangyin, also suffered losses due to speculative failures, owing 200,100 yuan to money shops such as Yongji Run in this county. The debt has been overdue for a long time. Yesterday, eight money shops, including Yongji Run, sent a letter to the Money Trade Association, which forwarded it to the national and provincial authorities, requesting the arrest and detention of Shen Jinqing and his two brothers, the owners of the firm, to ensure the recovery of the debt.

Private Trafficking of Draft Cattle Confiscated and Punished: The first detachment of the sixth team of the Second District of the Water Police stationed in Wuxi intercepted Yuan Mingdou, who was privately trafficking draft cattle, along with 61 head of cattle, in the Huangbu area. They were immediately transferred to the County Government for interrogation. However, the suspect carried a passport issued by the Danyang County Government, stating that according to the report submitted by Zhu Qikui, chairman of the Danyang Cattle Industry Association, on behalf of cattle merchants Zhu Ding and Zhu Ziyin, the 61 head of cattle were being transported to the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau for use in planting vaccine. County Magistrate Chen immediately submitted a request to the Department of Civil Affairs for instructions. It is now known that Director Zhao has approved the official letter from the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, stating that although the Danyang Dehua Public Welfare Two Cattle Firms were previously entrusted to purchase cattle, the order has long been terminated. After receiving the letter, Director Zhao determined that the cattle merchant was clearly engaged in private trafficking and specifically instructed the county government to confiscate all the cattle in accordance with Article 2 of the Provisional Regulations on Trafficking and Slaughtering Draft Cattle and impose a fine. As for the Danyang County Magistrate, who issued the passport improperly, a separate investigation will be conducted for disciplinary action.

Changshu

Latest News on the Kidnapping Case in Shazhou City: On the 16th of this month, over 20 bandits impersonating anti-smuggling team members in Xiaosha area, Changyinsha, Shazhou City, Fourth District of this county, first tied up and disarmed six members of the local security corps, then kidnapped Liu Defeng, Xue Wang, and one other person from nearby. It has been many days since the kidnapping and there has been no news of their whereabouts. Yesterday (the 23rd), two local gentry, Tang Jing'an and Zhang Jianliu, suddenly received a letter from Shanghai, presumably sent by the bandits. The letter stated that the three hostages are safe and sound in Shanghai, and asked them to inform their families to prepare the ransom and come to retrieve them. However, all the families of the hostages are extremely impoverished, and it's uncertain where such a large amount of money for ransom can be obtained. Hence, each of the families is in a state of extreme anxiety.

Changzhou

Inmate Attempted Jailbreak But Failed: Wu Guoguang, warden of the Wuyi Local Prison and head of the detention center, discovered inmate Guo Jinzhuang missing during a gate count at noon on the 24th. A search was immediately conducted, and Guo Jinzhuang, Zhong Shi, and Zhang Guiting were found hiding in a pile of straw in the North Cell's patrol route. A round hole was discovered at the base of the wall, prepared for a jailbreak attempt. After strict interrogation, they were shackled and reported to the county government for instructions. County Magistrate Zhang sent Qian Tangxin to inspect the site and sent a letter to the 155th Brigade Headquarters for further investigation. Brigade Commander Huang Gu was greatly angered and immediately brought the three soldiers back for interrogation. Zhong Shi and Guo Jinzhuang, who initiated the plan, were tied up and executed by firing squad at Fengweidun at around 10 AM this morning (the 25th).

Jiangyin

The Leader of the Jia Group Reports the Circumstances of Deserting Soldiers: Gu Xiting and others from Zhongzheng Township reported to the county government that Zou, the leader of the Second Jia Group, was hoarding and privately selling firearms, dereliction of duty, and harming the people. In particular, the attempt to seize deserting soldiers' firearms led to a conflict with the stationed army, and the firearms within the group were confiscated. County Magistrate Zou submitted his own defense, stating that on April 4th, over 20 deserting soldiers from a company of the first regiment of the 47th division stationed in Changshu were resisted and fled westward by the Yangku Security Group. On the morning of the 5th, they reached Hucao Port. He intended to go there to resolve the situation as ordered, but because the deserting soldiers had grenades, they listened to others and fled. Later, the first division and fourth regiment dispatched troops to pursue them, but because the deserting soldiers had gone elsewhere, they blamed the Second Jia Group, confiscated the firearms of the group members, and took away 15 group members. After negotiations by the county government, the 8th and 9th companies of Wangdai Town were ordered to return the firearms. Later, Wang Xinghan, the company commander of the first battalion of the third regiment of the 47th division, also led three companies of soldiers from Hucao Port to track down the deserting soldiers and searched house by house. Fortunately, Ma Zao, the director of the group affairs, persuaded the company commander, and the next day, they led the team elsewhere. He spent 124 yuan on entertaining expenses, and these expenses have not been settled. The above facts show that there was no intention to seize the firearms of the deserting soldiers or cause a conflict.

The West Bank of Ershilipu Collapsed Again: The west bank of Ershilipu in this county had already been completed, but after yesterday's rain, suddenly over 300 zhang collapsed. It is heard that the section chief of that section has already begun repairing it.

Boatman Drowned While Swimming: At Wangjiagang, District 11 of this county, a grass boat was docked the day before yesterday. There were three boatmen on the boat. Because it was hot in the afternoon, they agreed to go swimming in the river. Because they were in the water for too long, they drowned. Fortunately, many people rescued them, but only two were rescued. One person drowned.

They went to arrest him and found a pistol and ammunition inside the statue. There were also over 20 pairs of wet shoes. Xiaoshan

Serious Flooding in Shahe Township: Shahe Township, Fourth District of Xiaoshan, is surrounded by mountains on all sides and has low-lying land. Early rice is planted every year before the summer solstice and harvested in early autumn. Recently, due to continuous moldy rain, mountain floods have overflowed, and all 30,000 mu of farmland in the entire township have been submerged. The disaster has already occurred, and the general farmers are sending telegrams requesting relief. It is unknown how the superiors will handle it.

Educational News Highlights

Military Training for Three Weeks in High Schools and Above During Summer Vacation

Nanjing, 25th: The Ministry of Education has telegraphed all national universities, colleges, and provincial and municipal education departments to implement three weeks of extremely strict military training in all high schools and above during the summer vacation. Ministry of Education Orders Provinces and Cities to Establish Compulsory Education Starting Next Year

| First Phase and Short Term |

Nanjing, 25th: The Ministry of Education has ordered all provinces and cities to begin implementing the first phase of compulsory education and short-term compulsory education starting in 1932. If they cannot be implemented simultaneously, short-term compulsory education should be prioritized. A plan should be drafted and submitted to the Ministry for approval and implementation within one month.

Sports

Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation Cables the Olympic Committee Requesting Accommodations to Participate

Once the Committee Approves,

Liu Can Depart

After the announcement that the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation had decided not to send athletes to the World Games, the Japanese immediately used their manipulative tactics to spread propaganda in the newspapers, hoping to sow discord among the Chinese. Given our country's current difficult situation, it seems that sending athletes to the World Games is indispensable to maintain our international standing. The Federation, therefore, intends to send Liu Changchun alone to the Games. On the 13th, they telegraphed Chairman Zhang Boling and Chairman Wang Zhengting to decide. After discussion, Zhang and Wang obtained the energetic support of Hao Gengsheng, former Director of Physical Education at Northeastern University, who raised considerable funds in Tianjin and Peking to send Liu Changchun and Xi Weiyi as representatives to the Games, intending to restrain the Japanese and create a highlight in the history of Chinese sports. Hao telegraphed Chief Editor Shen Siliang with the revised plan the day before yesterday, but Shen, because all preparations were already in place, could not change the itinerary within a few hours. Therefore, he did not consider it. Now that this plan has become a likely reality, the Federation has urgently telegraphed the Olympic Committee, requesting permission to participate (the registration deadline was June 18th). Liu will depart as soon as the Committee approves.

The World Games Does Not Permit the Pseudo-State to Participate

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Claims That the Swiss General Assembly Did Not Approve: Nanjing, 25th (Central News Agency): This year's World Games will be held in the United States next month. It was previously reported that Japan intended to participate in the name of a rebel organization in Northeastern China. According to news from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the participating representatives of that organization must be approved by the Swiss General Assembly. The representatives selected by the rebels have not been approved, so they cannot attend the Games.

Although Few, the Filipino Olympians Will Surely Win

Hope for Tolibia as a High Jump Champion

Ite Fangsha is Sure to Win in Breaststroke

Manila, November 11th (Correspondence): Seven elite athletes from the Philippines boarded the Ryuten Maru bound for America to participate in the Olympics. The entire team consists of two coaches, one track and field athlete, three swimmers, and three boxers, all champions in Manila. Another boxer will board the Coolidge bound for America.

Track and Field: Tolibia is the only track and field athlete and the only hope for the Philippines to score points. At the 9th Games in Amsterdam, he tied for second place with France's Mannate and America's Hedges. He then competed for the ranking and finished fourth. Tolibia's height is 1.93 meters. The first place was won by America's Kimsey, who jumped over 2 meters at the Games, so there is great hope.

Swimming: Although there are only three swimmers, they are also sure to win. Ite Fangsha, Jackillin, and Ajerotin have repeatedly broken the world record of Japan's Takeda in the 200-meter breaststroke. The three of them all have times within 2 minutes and 47 seconds, while Takeda's record is 2 minutes 48.5 seconds. At the 9th Games, Ite Fangsha ranked third, Takeda was the champion, and La Dimaque (Germany) was second. Germany's Sius, Canada's Smith, and Sweden's Haling are all students of Ite. Ajerotin has not participated in the Olympics, but in the 9th Far East Games, both of them defeated Takeda in the breaststroke. Recently, the two have improved further, so they will surely win in Los Angeles.

China Youth Overwhelms McLing

| 104 to 64 Points |

Excellent Performance This Year's Great Harvest

Pole Vault and Javelin Break National Records

In yesterday's track meet between China Youth and McLing, China Youth overwhelmed McLing with a score of 104 to 64. The results in each event were outstanding, making it a great harvest for the track and field community this year.

Excellent Results

Lu Yaxiong's triple jump of 44 feet 2 inches is remarkable. The pole vault performance is even more surprising, reaching 11 feet 9 inches, equivalent to more than 3.60 meters. The champion was McLing's Si Huanke, whose height far exceeds the Chinese national record. McLing's Heitesheng's javelin also broke the Chinese national record, reaching 154 feet 2 inches, equivalent to more than 46 meters. Galundin's discus throw of 35.86 meters was also quite good. On the China Youth side, in addition to Lu Yaxiong's triple jump, Tao Yingjie's 400-meter hurdles in 54.75 seconds, Sun Huifei's long jump of 6.50 meters, Xia Xianmo's 800 meters in 2 minutes 12.6 seconds, and Xiao Dinghua's high hurdles in 17.2 seconds were all above-average performances.

China Youth Fought to the End

The competition started at 1:30 PM, with over a thousand spectators, full of enthusiasm and a strong competitive spirit. Both sides were highly motivated and did not slacken at all. The competition in the 100-meter, 200-meter, and 400-meter races was particularly fierce. McLing's Jianjiang Tangsleigh was slow off the mark and finished third in the 100-meter race. Hao Chunde and Zeng Rongzhong fought hard but failed in the 200-meter race. Zeng Rongzhong had excellent form in the 400-meter race, leading throughout the first 300 meters, but was overtaken by Blong in the last 100 meters, finishing a meter behind after a hard fight. The competition in the 1600-meter race was particularly interesting. Zhu Shaohua worked hard in the front but failed in the end. McLing's Shandun was a famous runner in this event and eventually won the championship. Dong Jiaxi had a fierce competition with Shandun but finished second by two meters. Xiao Dinghua's high hurdle form was extremely beautiful, worthy of a famous athlete.

Pole Vault Was Really Good

Cao Yu's pole vault and Chen Baoshen's 16-pound shot put were also above-average performances. Although Cao Yu finished second, his performance was still as good as before. Si Huanke's 11 feet 9 inches was something that Chinese athletes had never achieved before. Wang Jihuai only maintained his original state, neither improving nor declining. He won four second places in long jump, triple jump, javelin, and discus.

Comparison of Points Scored by Both Sides

After the 14 events, China Youth won eight first places, ten second places, and eight third places, totaling 104 points according to the 6-4-2 scoring system. McLing won six first places, four second places, and six third places, totaling 64 points.

Wang Jihuai had the highest individual score with four second places totaling 16 points. McLing's Galundin won one first place and one second place, totaling 10 points, and finished second overall. Chen Baoshen, Xiao Dinghua, Lu Yaxiong, Shan Mai, Sun Huifei, Tao Yingjie, and Cao Yu all had 8 points and finished third overall. The complete results are listed below.

Free Talk

Two-One Technical Talk

Extraordinary and Terrible

—

Why has our country not progressed? Why is politics not on track? There are thousands of problems, which cannot be fully explained in this small box of this column! Helplessly, I can only say a few key points:

(1) There are too few extraordinary people and too many terrible people!

(2) Once there is an extraordinary person, many terrible people will echo and rise up!

(3) The few extraordinary people are surrounded by the majority of terrible people; as a result, the extraordinary people are dissolved in the furnace of the terrible and undergo assimilation!

I can briefly explain the above examples one by one:

(1) Special people in the eyes of the public, shocked and amazed, are called extraordinary! Or, extraordinarily popular! Or, extraordinarily rich! Or, extraordinarily famous! Conversely, inept people in the eyes of the public, pitied and despised, are called terrible! Or, terribly black! Or, terribly poor! Or, terribly listless! If we compare the number of extraordinary and terrible people, it is difficult to find one extraordinary person in a thousand, while there are nine hundred ninety-nine and a half terrible people in a thousand.

(2) Once there is an extraordinary person, many terrible relatives and old friends come to attach themselves, climb the dragon, rely on the grass, and cling to the trees; surrounding this extraordinary person layer upon layer with many terrible relatives and old friends!

(3) Suppose, the extraordinary person aims to maintain his extraordinary honor; he must break through the layers of terrible! However, breaking through is not easy. To put it mildly: the encirclement of friends can be broken through; but the terribleness of relatives cannot be broken through! To put it more mildly: the encirclement of parents and family can be broken through; but the terribleness of cronyism cannot be broken through! Because of this, the extraordinary honor is dissolved in the furnace of the terrible and undergoes assimilation! What was extraordinary before has now become terrible!

The sharp decrease in the extraordinary and the surge in the terrible, how can society progress? How can politics get on track? Alas! This has become a terrible Republic of China!

The Tragic Death of the Outcast Wang Jihong

— Mian Zi

In Shanghai a few years ago, whenever there were musical gatherings, one could always hear Wang Jihong's pipa. His superb skills and silent demeanor, when mentioned, may evoke memories and leave some shadows in the minds of some people. Since the love triangle occurred, the sound of the pipa abruptly stopped. Now it has become an absolute silence, which cannot but make people sigh with sorrow. His death was truly tragic. When the January 28th Incident occurred in Shanghai, because of his love for the beauty of nature, he drifted to the Zhusha Temple on Huangshan Mountain in Anhui to live, enjoying the strange, beautiful, and magnificent scenery. Who knew that he, suffering from pulmonary tuberculosis, would pass away in the deep mountains and ancient temples due to poor nutrition and environment. He died in poverty, without relatives or friends. An old monk was the one who took care of his burial. When this news spread, everyone who knew him in life felt sadness, especially those friends who spent every day with him, who felt even more grief and were on the verge of tears.

He was a very intelligent young man who had conducted in-depth research on Chinese and Western music and literature. He truly possessed artistic talent, but unfortunately, he was arrogant, devoted himself to nature, and was not used by the world, causing him to be buried and to die with regret. China's Manshu and Europe's Byron both died young. He also had some similarities. How sad.

Regarding music, he composed a song called "Full City of Wind and Rain," which contained a sad and慷慨 melody and the sound of a storm. Now it has disappeared with him. He did not have any great works in literature, only two collections of new poems, "You Lan Girl" and "Qian Yun." Last year, when he was convalescing in Huangshan for the second time, he wrote ten miscellaneous seven-character poems, which were mournful and beautiful, and movingly poignant. They were published in a travel magazine, but alas, he did not even know they were published when he died. Some of his other articles were scattered in newspapers and magazines for a period of time. Later, he devoted himself to studying Buddhism and stopped writing. His unique life was very literary. The reporter knows it very well and plans to publish a special collection for him in the future. I also hope that readers can give me some information about him. Mr. Lu Erkui, who compiled the Ciyuan dictionary, Mr. Zheng Jinwen of the Datong Music Society, and playwright Ouyang Yuqian are all acquaintances of his. I wonder what their feelings are after receiving this sad news.

Amber's Origin in Guo Zan

— Tao Zaidong

Old Man Ninety-Three announced Mr. Cao Zhongyuan's letter, as seen in the 19th issue of this publication. The letter stated that a book by an Englishman, "The Precursors of Wireless Telegraphy," quoted Guo Pu of the Jin Dynasty on amber picking up mustard seeds. Mr. Cao explored which book Guo's words came from for many years without success. The sprouts of physics, electrochemistry, and science are often seen in Chinese ancient books, but there are very few inventions. Seeking the origin of the words is also meaningless. However, such words as "amber picking up mustard seeds" and "magnet attracting iron" are commonly seen in literary collections after the Tang and Song dynasties. It can be said that the Englishman traced the source. It is shameful that foreigners can quote it, but our people do not know its origin. Mr. Cao has been searching for years, and his diligence is admirable. We should write down what we know to help him. According to my research, this is a sentence from Guo Pu's "Annotations and Praises to the Classic of Mountains and Seas." Checking the "Yuanjian Leihan, Treasures Section," it adds a quote from Guo Pu's praise: "Magnets attract iron, amber picks up mustard seeds. Images have potential connections, and numbers also have hidden meetings. The mutual attraction of things is unexpected," and so on. Also, checking Guo Pu's most prominent works, besides annotating the Erya, is the "Annotations and Praises to the Classic of Mountains and Seas." Now that the "Yuanjian Leihan" has added a quote from Guo's praise, it is undoubtedly from the "Annotations and Praises to the Classic of Mountains and Seas." However, Guo's original book has been lost. It is unknown to me whether later generations have compiled versions. The quote in the "Yuanjian Leihan" is also quoted from various books since the Tang and Song dynasties. In addition to Guo's praise, I remember that "Baopuzi" certainly has the sentence "Magnets attract needles, amber picks up mustard seeds." Also, "amber lampwick, friction to treat wind," is mentioned in the annotations to the "Compendium of Materia Medica" or the "Thousand Gold Prescriptions," but my memory is not accurate. I have no books with me and cannot verify. In short, Ge Hong, Tao Hongjing, and Sun Simiao are all people of the Jin Dynasty, so it can be seen that these two things were commonly known in the Jin Dynasty and became common sayings at that time. The "Annotations to the Book of Changes" by Wang Bi quoted by Old Man Ninety-Three, as seen in the 20th issue of this publication, is from Wang Bi, who lived between the Han and Jin Dynasties. It is only natural that the origin of the words is from the Han Dynasty.

What I Expect from Mothers

— Idle Person

Mother, you gave birth to many men who talk and create great careers, but why do you also give birth to many female tumors of society? This is too unfair.

Regardless of whether they are men or women, they are all born from the mother's womb and should enjoy the same education from their parents and equal treatment from society, so that they can jointly shoulder the responsibility of the family and the obligations of social undertakings.

Society is the structure of humanity, and humanity is the combination of the two sexes, male and female. To support this precarious situation where society is about to collapse, the foundation of society must be strengthened.

Mother, you are the first person responsible for educating children. How should you educate children to eradicate the weakness of women who want to control power? How should you awaken your daughters' self-awareness? They should be ashamed of dependence and labor for their own lives.

Mother! I hope you educate your children to strive to create a bright history of mankind and teach them to use the surplus value of labor to help the old, young, sick, and suffering people in society!

World Tidbits

— Sea Traveler

In a prison in Colombo, Ceylon, there are three ferocious criminals, as fiery as fire and as strong as oxen, with extremely bad conduct. The prison officials could not manage them, so they were imprisoned in a particularly strong prison cell. Who knew that the bricks on all four sides of the iron window had been eaten by termites over time and could be pushed loose. It benefited these three criminals, who escaped without a trace.

There is an education expert in the United States who conducted an interesting experiment. He subjected his own ten-month-old son and a two-month-old chimpanzee to the same training. After various experimental methods, according to him, the chimpanzee was smarter and easier to train than the child. The child's advantage was only in learning to speak, and everything else was inferior to the chimpanzee.

More than 1.2 million people visit the library of the British Museum every year. The bookshelves are sixty miles long and contain four million volumes. It can be said to be a magnificent sight.

Pilgrimage on the Beijing-Hangzhou Canal (Part 2)

— Shanshan

(5) Glimpses of Huzhou From the car, Huzhou is a tranquil place, a paradise of tranquility that makes people feel comfortable, although that is not entirely the case in reality.

Among the telegraph poles, which are dense at times and sparse at others, are occasionally mixed one or two chimneys, with black snake-like smoke coming out of the chimney opening. The city walls are short, the buildings are simple, and at a glance, you can see dark roof backs. There are no red houses or multi-story buildings. Next to a small bridge, there is a small teahouse. A small awning boat swims under the bridge. There are no mountains for miles around, and the sky and the ground are equally vast. There are not many figures in the fields or at the end of the alleys. The air is tame and peaceful.

An elderly woman, carrying a bamboo basket, walked to the car window, raised her wrinkled head, and called out in a trembling voice, "Spiced tea eggs." (6) A Calm Mountain

In front of Lijia Lane, there is a mountain. No, I should say it is an incomparably huge stone. The color of this stone is aged green and humorous brown. The top of the stone is a diamond-shaped undulation. Among the mountains, it is the most robust and calm, with the temperament of the northern mountains. The mountain stones are clean. Many workers are mining stones on the side of the mountain. In the clanging sound of iron and stone colliding, we can taste the workers' sweat.

(7) Changing Cars in Changxing Because after Changxing is the territory of Jiangsu, the cars of the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau stop in Changxing. At that time, if you want to go further, you have to change cars. The car is from the Jiangnan Automobile Company. The vehicles are newer than those of the Provincial Highway Bureau, and they also seem wider. When I got on, it was already full of people. There was no way but to sit on the edge of a fat woman, which was very uncomfortable. (8) By the Side of Taihu Lake

After eleven o'clock, the car drove out of Changxing. Not long after, it arrived at the edge of Taihu Lake. The road meanders along the foot of the mountain. The mountains are towering and layered, like giant palms covering half of the sky. And the water in Taihu Lake? I really don't know how to describe its vastness. Engine fans and sails float in the vast water vapor. The end of the water is connected to the sky, making a very obvious contrast with the layered mountains that cover half of the sky. I felt like I was walking on the boundary between the ocean and the continent. My eyes were busy, constantly looking left and right.

(9) Black Columns of Smoke The car passed Jiapu and had already reached the territory of Yixing, Jiangsu. The countryside of Yixing produces pottery. The villagers build kilns on small hills and burn them every day. Black columns of smoke rise from the top of the mountain, growing larger and larger. Comparing this to cooking smoke, it seems that cooking smoke is not as scary. Comparing this to the magma when a volcano erupts, this column of smoke lacks a bit of strength.

(10) Escaped Cattle Since entering the territory of Yixing, the road changed from being covered with yellow sand to a gravel road, and the bridges also became wooden. Even though the vehicles were newer than those in Zhejiang, the road was uneven, bumping terribly. The passengers were violently shaken, as if the strength to breathe had been taken away.

The locals say that this bumpy car is an escaped ox, and the passengers have become watermelons being tossed about.

A Record of Dwelling with Both War and Peace (90)

— Owner of the Hall of Seeking Happiness

Chapter Eleven: Looking Up at the Commander's Banner in a Small and Remote Town; a Crowd of Vulgar People Follows the Attendants

Since the old man personally led these two honored officials to come, he would naturally have to accompany them to the Changxing Grand Hotel, his favorite place, so as to do his best to prepare a thoughtful and proper reception. Sure enough, the group galloped to the entrance of the Changxing Grand Hotel and stopped there. Fourth Master Wu was the first to jump off his horse, and with a beaming smile, he strode straight into the gate, repeatedly shouting, "Manager Qin, Manager Qin, come out and greet the guests." Fortunately, Manager Qin, with his earthy appearance, had already received the message and hurriedly opened the cash register, grabbed a neatly folded dark blue feather satin double-breasted waistcoat, unfolded it and put it on over his old blue coarse cloth lined robe. With two or three buttons still unfastened, he stumbled out and ran head-on into Fourth Master Wu at the accountant's counter inside the gate. Fourth Master Wu did not have time to speak slowly and deliberately. He grabbed Manager Qin's hand and ran out of the gate, pointing to a mule cart that had just stopped, and said, "I've brought two honored guests from the province. Let me introduce them to you first, and then welcome the honored guests out of the car." At this time, an honored guest had already been helped out of the first mule cart by an orderly. Manager Qin timidly raised his head and saw that this honored guest was actually a very handsome young military officer, wearing a brand new khaki military uniform. His whole body showed several very neat fold marks. Hanging on his shoulders were a pair of signs woven with small red-gold threads, surrounded by a rectangular gold border about one inch wide, with a star the size of a broad bean embedded in the middle, dazzling the eyes with its golden brilliance. Furthermore, with that one stride, it was discovered that the heels of his pair of shiny, new, tall, yellow leather boots were also fitted with gold spurs. Even if the foot landed with a thud on the ash heap in the incense-burner-like street, it could not bury the shimmering of the golden light. This caused Manager Qin, who was accustomed to doing business, to be filled with an indescribable surprise from the discerning eyes that recognized the precious value of gold. He secretly thought that this great person simply regarded gold as dirt. This was the first time this earthy old man had ever opened his eyes and seen such a sight. He was so dizzy that he lost his mind, drooled from the corners of his mouth, and stood there in a daze. Thanks to Fourth Master Wu waking him up in a leisurely manner in his ear, introducing him in such a loud voice, "Come, come, come. First meet our Commander An."

Foreign Exchange Turns from Flat to Loose

Yesterday, the silver market saw further contraction, with exchange rates slightly lower. The local market suddenly experienced a change of sentiment. HSBC's listed rates, except for the French franc which decreased by one yuan, remained unchanged. However, internally, the market shifted from flat in the morning to loose later. This caused gold prices to show a rebound, creating a confusing situation. Comparing the closing prices with the previous day, British gold was flat, while US dollars increased by 0.025. The volume of transactions by Chinese merchants was less than the previous day, with British gold transactions totaling approximately 100,000 pounds. Gold traders engaged in "digging far, releasing near," buying October contracts from Bombay. US dollar transactions amounted to approximately 500,000 to 600,000 yuan, mostly buying to cover short positions, with some selling gold to settle accounts at a price about six taels lower than yesterday, around 70 taels. Fluctuating Cotton Yarn Market Turns More Favorable

The cotton yarn market has improved, and the situation is extremely chaotic, changing three times a day, making it difficult to grasp. This is mainly due to the prolonged decline in prices, from 156 taels to 39 taels. Rongxinghao alone bought heavily for two days, turning from short to long. In the morning, news that the US was likely to extend credit for cotton purchases to China caused panic in the market, with prices plummeting by two taels, breaking through 40 taels. Selling pressure was intense, but then a large firm bought in, leading to a rebound and pushing prices above 40 taels. The afternoon situation remained tense. Currently, the market is in a turbulent state, with rapid changes. However, actual demand remains sluggish. Overall, the economic downturn has severely affected yarn sales. Most traders expect the price of standard yarn to return to around 145 taels.

Fluctuations in Standard Yarn Trading: In the morning session of standard yarn trading, prices fell by two taels across all months due to news that the US was likely to extend credit for cotton purchases, causing market panic and increasing the number of sellers. However, prices rebounded at the close, with all months rising by 0.05, 0.06, and 0.09 taels. In the afternoon session, news that a certain country's yarn had fallen by 3 to 4 yuan caused the market to weaken slightly. Last Week's US Cotton Market Firm Due to Insect Infestation

Good Cotton Crop in the East, Poor in the West. New York, June 24th: A report on the cotton market for the week states that the cotton market has rebounded from recent low records, with market prices fluctuating considerably and trading being quiet. Occasional showers in the eastern cotton belt have increased concerns about boll weevil infestations. While this concern has not triggered strong buying, it has limited selling. There is no pressure to sell from the South, so sales have been limited. Recent sunny and hot weather in the East has slightly increased selling. Many July futures have been closed out, absorbed by trade purchases and short covering at lower prices. Reports from the western cotton belt indicate good cotton crops. Some believe that excessive rainfall in the East, along with reports of excessive cotton leaf sap and weeds in cotton fields, and the spread of boll weevils in two-thirds of the southern cotton belt from Louisiana eastward, will offset the good cotton crop in the West. Some believe the spread of boll weevils is very serious, the worst since 1923. The weekend statistics are appended below (units of 1,000 bales):

However, rapid increases may also face setbacks, as pressure from hedging may be exerted after calculating the cost of foreign wheat.
